     <div class="sidebar__widget-item widget_school_closings" id="school_closings-2">
      <script>
       jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
                function handleSuccess(response) {
                    let closings = $(response).find('NUM_CLOSINGS');
                    if (closings.length === 0) {
                        return;
                    }

                    let num_closing = parseInt(closings.text());
                    $('.sidebar__school-closings__count').html(num_closing);
                    if (num_closing === 0) {
                        $('.sidebar__school-closings__link').css({'background-color': '#1e73be'});
                    }
                    else {
                        $('.sidebar__school-closings__link').css({'background-color': '#c10000'});
                    }
                }

                $.ajax({
                    method: 'GET',
                    url: 'https://week.assets.quincymedia.com/newsticker/closings.xml',
                    crossDomain: true,
                    dataType: 'xml',
                    success: handleSuccess,
                    error: function (error) {
                        console.error('SCHOOL CLOSINGS GET ERROR', error);
                    }
                });
            });
      </script>
